<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головка.html>голо́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головка.html>голо́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головка.html>голо́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головка.html>голо́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small head</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>head <i>(of pin, hammer, nail, etc.)</i></li>
<li>bulb, clove <i>(onion, garlic, etc.)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> glans penis</li></ol>

***головной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a> (8787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golvьnъ</i>. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golovnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:платок.html>плато́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golovnój</b> platók</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>head</b>scarf</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:головной.html>головно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мозг.html>мозг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golovnój</b> mozg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cerebrum</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>head</b> brain</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>main, principal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:головня.html>головня́</a> (20099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golvьna</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головня.html>головня́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golovnjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головня.html>головни́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головня.html>головни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головня.html>головне́й</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:головокружение.html>головокруже́ние</a> (8559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golová</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружение.html>круже́ние</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kružénije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whirling, spinning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головокружение.html>головокруже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golovokružénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головокружение.html>головокруже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головокружение.html>головокруже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:головокружение.html>головокруже́ний</a></b>)

***головоломка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:головоломка.html>головоло́мка</a> (28618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></b> (head) + stem of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></b> (to break) + suffix -к-
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лод</a> (1871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">голодъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golodŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*goldъ</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голодание.html>голода́ние</a> (16513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодать.html>голода́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golodátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодание.html>голода́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golodánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодание.html>голода́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодание.html>голода́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодание.html>голода́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***голодный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a> (17181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*goldьnъ</i>; synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólod</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hunger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">гало́дны</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">halódny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golódnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)голодне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)голодне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hungry, starving</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> famine, starveling, starvation, hunger
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бунт.html>бунт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golódnyj</b> bunt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">revolt of the hungry, starvelings' revolt</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golódnaja</b> smertʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starvation</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>meagre, scanty, poor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golódnyj</b> god</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lean year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:паек.html>паёк</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golódnyj</b> pajók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">starvation rations</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golódnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дных</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дная</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hungry person, starving person</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодовка.html>голодо́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golodóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодовка.html>голодо́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодовка.html>голодо́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодовка.html>голодо́вок</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́ха</a> (19634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лод</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golodúxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (prolonged)  hunger, starvation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голодуха.html>голоду́хи</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>golodúxi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">out of hunger, due to hunger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***голос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a> (148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">голосъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golosŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">voice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golsъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">voice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic without pleophony.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gólos</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лоса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голоса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голосо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>voice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горловой.html>горлово́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gorlovój <b>gólos</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">guttural <b>voice</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петушиный.html>петуши́ный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">petušínyj <b>gólos</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">squeaky <b>voice</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внезапно.html>внеза́пно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:умолк.html>умо́лк</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Gólos</b> vnezápno umólk.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>The voice</b> suddenly stopped.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>voice, word, remark, opinion
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v odín <b>gólos</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">unanimously, with one accord</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>vote
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́во</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лоса</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">právo <b>gólosa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">suffrage, the vote, franchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">постановля́ть/<a href = vnd.unilang:постановить.html>постанови́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большинство.html>большинство́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голосо́в</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">postanovljátʹ/postanovítʹ bolʹšinstvóm <b>golosóv</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resolve by a majority of votes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***голосование.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́ние</a> (8832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосовать.html>голосова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golosovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golosovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>voting, poll, polling</li>
<li>hitchhiking <i>(from raising a hand as if voting)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голосовать.html>голосова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golosovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проголосовать.html>проголосова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to vote <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">assert a formalised choice</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***голубеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубеть.html>голубе́ть</a> (10267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golubój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубеть.html>голубе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golubétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поголубе́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show blue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубеть.html>голубе́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>горы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí <b>golubéli</b> gory</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the mountains showed blue in the distance; blue mountains loomed in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn blue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn gay <i>(homosexual)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golubój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glaz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубоглазый.html>голубогла́зый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">goluboglázyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>blue-eyed</li></ol>

***голубой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубой</a> (873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубь.html>го́лубь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólubʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pigeon, dove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as a bluish tint of neck plumage.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golubój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)голубе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:голубь.html>голубе́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">голубе́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>light blue, sky blue, cyan, azure <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">contrast <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sínij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark blue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><table><tbody><tr><td>blue color: </td><td bgcolor="ADD8E6" width="80"> </td></tr></tbody></table></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экран.html>экра́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubój</b> ekrán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">television, TV set</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́голь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubój</b> úgolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wind power</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:песец.html>песе́ц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubój</b> peséc</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blue fox</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гигант.html>гига́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Golubój</b> gigánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Big Blue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubój</b> šum</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blue noise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:газ.html>газ</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubój</b> gaz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">water gas</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятно.html>пятно́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubóje</b> pjatnó</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Locus_ceruleus" class="extiw" title="w:Locus ceruleus">Locus ceruleus</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голуба́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubája</b> mečtá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">secret dream; a dream that one can never realize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голуба́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кровь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>golubája</b> krovʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blue blood; aristocrat, member of the royal family</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принц.html>принц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́ви</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">princ <b>golubój</b> króvi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prince</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">prince of blue blood</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gay, homosexual
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></b> мью́зикл.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My xodíli na <b>golubój</b> mʹjúzikl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We went to [see] a gay musical.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golubój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sínij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (different shades of blue) name distinct basic colors in Russian, as different from each other as blue and green would be for an English speaker; Russian does not have one single color term corresponding to "blue".</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golubój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубы́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубы́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gay (neutral term, see also <a href = vnd.unilang:гей.html>гей</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:педераст.html>педера́ст</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:гомосексуалист.html>гомосексуалист</a>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голубо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golubók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голубка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голубки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голубко́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голу́бка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубь.html>го́лубь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólubʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: young pigeon, dove</li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубок.html>голу́бок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golúbok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>

***голый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>го́лый</a> (1182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*galw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked, bald</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">callow</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">goły</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kahl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">calvo</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">کل</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>го́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gólyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)голе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)голе́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>го́лый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>naked, nude, bare</li>
<li>poor, miserable</li></ol>
